---
about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> This lecture introduces
  the hyperboloic paraboloid, hyparhedra, and the circular pleat. Topics include triangulated
  folding of the hypar, how paper folds between creases, and Gaussian curvature. Various
  proofs involving straight creases are given.</p> <p><strong>Speaker:</strong> Erik
  Demaine</p>
course_id: 6-849-geometric-folding-algorithms-linkages-origami-polyhedra-fall-2012
